===============

 on May 29, 2016

* [Decklists](#decklists)
* [Standings](#standings)

Bracket
-------





### Quarterfinals






**(1) Collecter, 2-1**






 (8) Mr. Random 







**(4) Montolio, 2-1**






 (5) Lexor19 







**(2) Call1Me1Dragon, 2-0**






 (7) JdPhoenix

**(1) Collecter, 2-1**






 (4) Montolio

 (3) Pubert 







### Finals






**(1) Collecter, 2-0**






 (2) Call1Me1Dragon
